# Shadow Bot Experiment Log

Tracks all 44 shadow bot monitoring snapshots and records the live deployment decision when a winner is auto-deployed.

---

## Experiment Setup

**Started:** 2026-03-25 ~06:35 ET
**Purpose:** Find optimal parameter combination for live Kalshi crypto trading
**Starting balance per bot:** $244.70 (24,470¢)
**Live deploy uses:** 50% of real Kalshi balance as working bankroll (scales dynamically)

### Parameter Grid — 44 Bots

| Dimension | Values tested |
|-----------|--------------|
| Win prob threshold | 0.60, 0.65, 0.70 |
| Edge floor (¢) | 0, 1–10, 0 |
| Kelly fraction | 0.10, 0.15, 0.25, 0.35, 0.50, 0.60, 0.75, 0.90, 1.00 |

**Kelly sweep anchor:** WP=0.65, Edge=5¢, KF=AN(0.10)/AP(0.15)/U(0.25)/AQ(0.35)/AE(0.50)/AR(0.60)/AL(0.75)/AS(0.90)/AO(1.00)

### Auto-Deploy Criteria

A winner is deployed automatically when ALL four conditions are met:

1. **≥300 settled trades** — enough sample size to be statistically meaningful
2. **≥60% win rate** — must be genuinely predictive
3. **Profitable** — net positive P&L (balance > $244.70 start)
4. **Beats ≥4 bots** by profit-per-trade, where each beaten bot has ≥100 settled trades

Ranked by **profit-per-trade** (P&L ÷ settled trades), not raw P&L — prevents high-frequency low-edge bots from winning by volume alone.

### Monitoring Schedule

- **Snapshot:** every 5 min → `/tmp/shadow_monitor.log`
- **Auto-deploy eval:** every 15 min → `/tmp/shadow_deploy.log` on deployment
- **This file:** appended on every snapshot + updated on live deployment

---
